Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 163, the first (unflown) release of the Apollo 14 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with reconstructed source code for Luminary 173. Changes between revision 163 and 173 were backed out, as described by Luminary memos 157 and 158. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152N. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those for the baseline log section mentioned in each file's changelog; the page numbers for a real Luminary 163 listing would be different.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

021710,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021711,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021712,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary revision 163.
021713,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the first
021714,000006:                                                                                                  ##              (unflown) release of the flight software for the Lunar
021715,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 14.
021716,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a reconstructed copy of
021717,000009:                                                                                                  ##              Luminary 173, as well as Luminary memos 157 amd 158.
021718,000010:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
021719,000011:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 163 in NASA
021720,000012:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021152N, which gives relatively high confidence
021721,000013:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
021722,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 500-611
021723,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
021724,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021725,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021726,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-21 MAS  Created from Luminary 173. Removed setting and
021727,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              clearing of R12RDFLG from R12READ.

021730,000022:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021731,000023:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021732,000024:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021733,000025:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021734,000026:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021735,000027: 
021736,000028:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021737,000029:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021738,000030:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021739,000031:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021740,000032:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021741,000033: 
021742,000034:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021743,000035:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021744,000036:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
021745,000037:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
021746,000038:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
021747,000039:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
021748,000040:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021749,000041:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021750,000042:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
021751,000043:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
021752,000044:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
021753,000045:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021754,000046:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021755,000047:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021756,000048:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021757,000049:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021758,000050:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021759,000051:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021760,000052:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021761,000053:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021762,000054:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021763,000055:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
021764,000056:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021765,000057:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
021766,000058: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021767,000059: 
021768,000060: 33,2117                                           BANK     33                                    
021769,000061: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021770,000062: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021771,000063: 
021772,000064: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021773,000065: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021774,000066: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
021775,000067: 24,2000           05340        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG

022255,000547:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022256,000548:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022257,000549:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022258,000550:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022259,000551:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022260,000552: 
022261,000553:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022262,000554:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022263,000555:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022264,000556:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022265,000557:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022266,000558:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022267,000559:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022268,000560:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022269,000561:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022270,000562:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022271,000563:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022272,000564:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022273,000565:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022274,000566:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022275,000567:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022276,000568:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022277,000569:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022278,000570:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022279,000571:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022280,000572:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022281,000573:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022282,000574:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022283,000575: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022284,000576: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022285,000577: 24,2462           05340        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022286,000578: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022287,000579: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022288,000580: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022289,000581: 
022290,000582: 24,2466           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022291,000583: 24,2467           11241                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022292,000584: 24,2470           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022293,000585: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022294,000586: 24,2472           05515                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022295,000587: 24,2473           00006                           ADRES    P25FLAG                               #  SET P25FLAG
022296,000588: 24,2474           05527                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              
022297,000589: 24,2475           00010                           ADRES    RNDVZFLG                              
022298,000590: 24,2476           05364        P25LEM1            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022299,000591: 24,2477           04022                           OCT      04022

022301,000593: 24,2501           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 #  IS P25FLAG SET
022302,000594: 24,2502           00006                           EXTEND

022304,000596: 24,2504           34747                           CAF      TRACKBIT                              #  IS TRACKFLAG SET?

Page 512 

022306,000598: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1                         
022307,000599: 24,2506           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022308,000600: 24,2507           12515                           BZF      P25LMWT1                              #  NO-SKIP PHASE CHANGE AND WAIT 1 MINUTE
022309,000601: 24,2510           34757                           CAF      SEVEN                                 #  CALL R65 - FINE PREFERRED
022310,000602: 24,2511           55745                           TS       R65CNTR                               
022311,000603: 24,2512           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE
022312,000604: 24,2513           46123                           CADR     R65LEM

022327,000619:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022328,000620:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022329,000621:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022330,000622:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022331,000623:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022332,000624: 
022333,000625:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022334,000626:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022335,000627:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022336,000628:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022337,000629:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022338,000630:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022339,000631:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
022340,000632:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
022341,000633:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
022342,000634:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022343,000635:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022344,000636:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022345,000637:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
022346,000638:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022347,000639:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
022348,000640:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
022349,000641:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022350,000642:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
022351,000643:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022352,000644:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3

022531,000823:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
022532,000824:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022533,000825:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2

022535,000827:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022536,000828: 
022537,000829:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022538,000830:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022539,000831:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -

022739,001031:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2

022741,001033:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022742,001034: 
022743,001035:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022744,001036:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -

022750,001042:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23

022807,001099:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022808,001100:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022809,001101:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022810,001102:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022811,001103:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022812,001104: 
022813,001105:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022814,001106:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022815,001107:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022816,001108:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022817,001109:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
022818,001110:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
022819,001111:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
022820,001112:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
022821,001113:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022822,001114:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
022823,001115:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
022824,001116:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
022825,001117:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022826,001118:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
022827,001119:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022828,001120:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022829,001121:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022830,001122:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022831,001123:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022832,001124:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022833,001125:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022834,001126:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022835,001127:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022836,001128:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
022837,001129: 24,3272  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022838,001130: 24,3272                                           COUNT*   $$/R24

022842,001134: 24,3275           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21

022908,001200:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022909,001201:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022910,001202:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO : 3                      DATE : 4-11-67
022911,001203:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY : P VOLANTE  SDC
022912,001204: 
022913,001205: 
022914,001206:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-

023117,001409:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023118,001410: 
023119,001411:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023120,001412:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023121,001413:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023122,001414:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023123,001415:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023124,001416:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023125,001417:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023126,001418:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023127,001419:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023128,001420:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023129,001421:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023130,001422:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023131,001423:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023132,001424:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023133,001425:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023134,001426: 
023135,001427:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023136,001428:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023137,001429:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S   (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023138,001430: 
023139,001431:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023140,001432:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023141,001433:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023142,001434:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023143,001435: 
023144,001436:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023145,001437: 
023146,001438:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023147,001439: 
023148,001440:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023149,001441: 
023150,001442:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023151,001443:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023152,001444: 
023153,001445:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

023196,001488:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023197,001489: 
023198,001490:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023199,001491:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023200,001492:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023201,001493:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023202,001494:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023203,001495:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023204,001496:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023205,001497:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023206,001498:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023207,001499:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023208,001500:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023209,001501:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023210,001502:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023211,001503:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023212,001504:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023213,001505:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023214,001506:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023215,001507:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023216,001508:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023217,001509:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023218,001510: 
023219,001511:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023220,001512:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF
023221,001513: 
023222,001514:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
023223,001515:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
023224,001516: 
023225,001517:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023226,001518:

023266,001558:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023267,001559: 
023268,001560:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023269,001561: 
023270,001562:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023271,001563:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023272,001564:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023273,001565:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023274,001566:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023275,001567:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023276,001568:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023277,001569:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023278,001570:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023279,001571:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023280,001572:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023281,001573:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023282,001574: 
023283,001575:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023284,001576:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023285,001577:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023286,001578: 
023287,001579:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023288,001580:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023289,001581: 
023290,001582:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023291,001583: 
023292,001584:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023293,001585:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023294,001586: 
023295,001587:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023296,001588: 
023297,001589:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023298,001590: 
023299,001591: 24,3340                                           BANK     24                                    
023300,001592: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023301,001593: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023302,001594: 
023303,001595: 25,2073  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023304,001596: 25,2073                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023305,001597: 25,2073           02102        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023306,001598: 25,2074           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023307,001599: 25,2075           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.

023314,001606:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023315,001607: 
023316,001608:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023317,001609:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023318,001610:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023319,001611:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023320,001612:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023321,001613:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023322,001614:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023323,001615:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023324,001616:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023325,001617:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023326,001618:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023327,001619:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023328,001620:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023329,001621:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023330,001622:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023331,001623:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023332,001624: 
023333,001625:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023334,001626:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023335,001627:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023336,001628: 
023337,001629:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023338,001630: 
023339,001631:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023340,001632:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023341,001633: 
023342,001634:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
023343,001635: 
023344,001636:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023345,001637: 
023346,001638: 25,2102           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
023347,001639: 25,2103           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
023348,001640: 25,2104           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023349,001641: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023350,001642: 25,2106           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023351,001643: 25,2107           05232                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023352,001644: 25,2110           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023353,001645:

023387,001679:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023388,001680:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023389,001681:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023390,001682:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023391,001683:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023392,001684:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023393,001685:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023394,001686:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023395,001687:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023396,001688:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023397,001689:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023398,001690:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023399,001691:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023400,001692:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023401,001693:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023402,001694:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023403,001695:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
023404,001696:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
023405,001697:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
023406,001698:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023407,001699:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
023408,001700:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
023409,001701:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
023410,001702:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
023411,001703: 
023412,001704:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023413,001705:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
023414,001706:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
023415,001707: 
023416,001708:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023417,001709:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023418,001710: 
023419,001711:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023420,001712:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
023421,001713: 
023422,001714:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023423,001715:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023424,001716: 
023425,001717:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
023426,001718: 
023427,001719:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
023428,001720: 
023429,001721: 25,2140           02167        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
023430,001722:

023474,001766:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023475,001767: 
023476,001768:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023477,001769:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
023478,001770:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023479,001771:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023480,001772:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023481,001773:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023482,001774:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023483,001775:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023484,001776:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023485,001777:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023486,001778:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023487,001779:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023488,001780:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
023489,001781:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023490,001782:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023491,001783:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
023492,001784:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023493,001785:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023494,001786:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
023495,001787:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023496,001788: 
023497,001789:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023498,001790:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023499,001791:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023500,001792:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023501,001793:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
023502,001794: 
023503,001795:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023504,001796:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023505,001797: 
023506,001798:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023507,001799:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023508,001800: 
023509,001801:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023510,001802:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023511,001803: 
023512,001804:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023513,001805: 
023514,001806:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  STDESIG

023567,001859:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023568,001860: 
023569,001861:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023570,001862:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023571,001863:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
023572,001864:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023573,001865:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
023574,001866:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
023575,001867:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023576,001868:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023577,001869:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
023578,001870:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023579,001871:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
023580,001872:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023581,001873:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023582,001874:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023583,001875:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
023584,001876: 
023585,001877:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE*  (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023586,001878:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
023587,001879:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
023588,001880:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023589,001881:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023590,001882: 
023591,001883:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023592,001884:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023593,001885: 
023594,001886:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023595,001887:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023596,001888: 
023597,001889:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023598,001890:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023599,001891: 
023600,001892:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023601,001893: 
023602,001894:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023603,001895:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)
023604,001896:                                                                                                  #  L+1  (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)

023655,001947:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023656,001948: 
023657,001949:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023658,001950:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023659,001951:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023660,001952:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023661,001953:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023662,001954:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023663,001955:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023664,001956:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
023665,001957:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023666,001958:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023667,001959:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023668,001960:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023669,001961:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023670,001962:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023671,001963: 
023672,001964:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023673,001965:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023674,001966:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
023675,001967: 
023676,001968:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023677,001969:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
023678,001970:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
023679,001971:

023761,002053:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023762,002054: 
023763,002055:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023764,002056:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023765,002057:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023766,002058:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023767,002059:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023768,002060:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023769,002061:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023770,002062:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023771,002063:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023772,002064:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023773,002065:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023774,002066:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023775,002067:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023776,002068:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023777,002069:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023778,002070:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023779,002071:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023780,002072:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023781,002073:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023782,002074:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023783,002075:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023784,002076:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023785,002077:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023786,002078: 
023787,002079:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023788,002080:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023789,002081:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
023790,002082:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023791,002083:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023792,002084: 
023793,002085:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023794,002086:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
023795,002087: 
023796,002088:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023797,002089:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023798,002090:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
023799,002091: 
023800,002092:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023801,002093:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023802,002094: 
023803,002095:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023804,002096: 
023805,002097:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023806,002098:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023807,002099:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

023847,002139:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023848,002140: 
023849,002141:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023850,002142:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023851,002143:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023852,002144:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023853,002145:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023854,002146:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023855,002147:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023856,002148:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023857,002149:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023858,002150:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
023859,002151:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023860,002152:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
023861,002153:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023862,002154:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023863,002155:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023864,002156:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023865,002157:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023866,002158:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023867,002159:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023868,002160:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023869,002161:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023870,002162:

023872,002164:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
