024019,002311:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024020,002312: 
024021,002313:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024022,002314:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024023,002315:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024024,002316:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024025,002317:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024026,002318:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024027,002319:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024028,002320:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024029,002321:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024030,002322:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024031,002323:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024032,002324:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024033,002325:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024034,002326:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024035,002327:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024036,002328:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024037,002329:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024038,002330:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024039,002331:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024040,002332:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024041,002333:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024042,002334:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024043,002335:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024044,002336:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024045,002337:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024046,002338:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024047,002339: 
024048,002340:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024049,002341:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024050,002342:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024051,002343:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024052,002344: 
024053,002345:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024054,002346:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024055,002347: 
024056,002348:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024057,002349:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024058,002350: 
024059,002351:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024060,002352: 
024061,002353:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024062,002354:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024063,002355: 
024064,002356:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024065,002357:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024066,002358:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024067,002359: 
024068,002360: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024114,002406:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024115,002407: 
024116,002408:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024117,002409:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024118,002410:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024119,002411:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024120,002412:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024121,002413:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024122,002414:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024123,002415:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024124,002416:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024125,002417:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024126,002418:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024127,002419:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024128,002420:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024129,002421:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024130,002422:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024131,002423:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024132,002424:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024133,002425:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024134,002426:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024135,002427:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024136,002428:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024137,002429:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024138,002430:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024139,002431:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024140,002432:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024141,002433:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024142,002434:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024143,002435:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024144,002436:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024145,002437:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024146,002438:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024147,002439:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024148,002440:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024149,002441:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024150,002442:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024151,002443:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024152,002444:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024153,002445:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024154,002446: 
024155,002447:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024156,002448:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024157,002449: 
024158,002450:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024159,002451:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024160,002452:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024161,002453: 
024162,002454:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024163,002455:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024164,002456:

Page 557 

024166,002458:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024167,002459:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024168,002460: 
024169,002461:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024170,002462:

024442,002734:                                                                                                  #  RADAR RUPT READER (R20)
024443,002735: 
024444,002736:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE, WHICH IS INITIATED BY A RADAR RUPT, PROCESSES THE RADAR DATA AND UPDATES THE APPROPRIATE
024445,002737:                                                                                                  #  DSKY LIGHTS.
024446,002738: 
024447,002739: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   RADARUPT

024450,002742: 25,3174                                           COUNT*   $$/RRUPT

024453,002745: 
024454,002746: 25,3174           00006        RADAREAD           EXTEND                                         #  CONTINUATION OF INTERRUPT LEAD-IN.
024455,002747: 25,3175           04007                           ROR      SUPERBNK                              #  SUPERBNK MUST BE SAVED BECAUSE RUPT
024456,002748: 25,3176           54016                           TS       BANKRUPT                              #  MAY EXIT VIA TASKOVER.
024457,002749: 25,3177           00006                           EXTEND                                         
024458,002750: 25,3200           22012                           QXCH     QRUPT                                 
024459,002751: 
024460,002752: 
024461,002753: 25,3201           34757                           CA       SEVEN                                 #  READ AND STORE RADAR SELECT BITS
024462,002754: 25,3202           00006                           EXTEND

024465,002757: 
024466,002758: 25,3205           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  IF RADAR SELECT BITS ARE ZERO, ALARM
024467,002759: 25,3206           13214                           BZF      BADRUPT                               #  WITHOUT READING DATA
024468,002760: 
024469,002761: 25,3207           30046                           CA       RNRAD                                 #  STORE RAW DATA FOR DOWNLINK.
024470,002762: 25,3210           51332                           INDEX    RADBITS

024472,002764: 
024473,002765: 25,3212           11077                           CCS      RADUSE                                #  IF RADUSE IS ZERO, THIS IS A BAD RUPT
024474,002766: 25,3213           13220                           TCF      WHICHRAD                              
024475,002767:

025077,003369:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025078,003370:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025079,003371: 
025080,003372: 
025081,003373:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025082,003374: 
025083,003375:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025084,003376:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025085,003377:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025086,003378: 
025087,003379:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025088,003380: 
025089,003381: 
025090,003382:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025091,003383: 
025092,003384: 
025093,003385:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025094,003386: 
025095,003387:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
025096,003388:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025097,003389:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025098,003390:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025099,003391:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025100,003392: 
025101,003393: 
025102,003394:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025103,003395: 
025104,003396:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025105,003397:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025106,003398: 
025107,003399: 
025108,003400:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025109,003401:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025110,003402: 
025111,003403: 
025112,003404:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025113,003405:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025114,003406: 
025115,003407:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025116,003408: 
025117,003409:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025118,003410:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025119,003411:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025120,003412:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS

025325,003617:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
025326,003618:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
025327,003619:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
025328,003620: 
025329,003621:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025330,003622: 
025331,003623:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
025332,003624:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
025333,003625:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
025334,003626: 
025335,003627:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025336,003628:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
025337,003629:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
025338,003630:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
025339,003631:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
025340,003632:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
025341,003633:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
025342,003634: 
025343,003635: 
025344,003636:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025345,003637:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
025346,003638:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
025347,003639: 
025348,003640:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025349,003641:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025350,003642:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025351,003643:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025352,003644:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025353,003645:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025354,003646: 
025355,003647: 
025356,003648:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025357,003649:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025358,003650:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025359,003651:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025360,003652:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025361,003653:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
025362,003654:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
025363,003655:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
025364,003656:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
025365,003657:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
025366,003658:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
025367,003659:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
025368,003660:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
025369,003661:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
025370,003662:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025371,003663: 
025372,003664:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025373,003665:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
025374,003666:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

025766,004058:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025767,004059: 
025768,004060:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025769,004061:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025770,004062:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025771,004063: 
025772,004064:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025773,004065:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
025774,004066:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
025775,004067: 
025776,004068:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025777,004069:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025778,004070:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025779,004071:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025780,004072:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025781,004073:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025782,004074:

Page 596 

025784,004076:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025785,004077:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025786,004078:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025787,004079:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025788,004080:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025789,004081:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025790,004082:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025791,004083: 
025792,004084:

025839,004131: 
025840,004132:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE INITIALIZES THE W-MATRIX BY ZEROING ALL W THEN SETTING
025841,004133:                                                                                                  #  DIAGONAL ELEMENTS TO INITIAL STORED VALUES.

025989,004281:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025990,004282:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
025991,004283: 
025992,004284: 
025993,004285:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025994,004286: 
025995,004287:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025996,004288:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025997,004289:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025998,004290:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025999,004291: 
026000,004292: 
026001,004293:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026002,004294: 
026003,004295: 
026004,004296:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026005,004297: 
026006,004298:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026007,004299:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026008,004300:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026009,004301:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026010,004302:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026011,004303: 
026012,004304: 
026013,004305:                                                                                                  #  EXIT  - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026014,004306: 
026015,004307: 
026016,004308:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026017,004309: 
026018,004310:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026019,004311:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026020,004312:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026021,004313: 
026022,004314:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026023,004315:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026024,004316:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026025,004317:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026026,004318: 
026027,004319:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026028,004320:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026029,004321:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026030,004322:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026031,004323:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026032,004324: 
026033,004325: 
026034,004326: 26,3444                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24
